# 道藏目录详注

**Imperially Commissioned Siku Quanshu**
**Section on Classics (Zibu) – Volume 14: Detailed Catalog of the Daoist Canon (Daozang Mulu Xiangzhu)**

**Daoist Category – Summary**

The undersigned officials, having carefully examined the *Detailed Catalog of the Daoist Canon* in four volumes, compiled by the Ming Daoist monk Baiyun Xi (style name Mingzhi, courtesy name Zai Xu, a native of Shangyuan), note that this work was completed in the year Tianqi Bingyin (1626). The author systematically categorized the Daoist Canon by its textual traditions, dividing it into three primary *Dun* (caverns) and four auxiliary *Fu* (assistants), totaling twelve classifications.

The three *Dun* are:
1. **Dunzhēn (True Cavern)** – The teachings transmitted by the Primordial Sovereign Yuan Shi Tianzun, constituting the *Great Vehicle* of the highest law.
2. **Dunyuan (Elemental Cavern)** – The teachings transmitted by the Most High Laozi, constituting the *Middle Vehicle* of the middle law.
3. **Dunshén (Divine Cavern)** – Also originating from the Most High Laozi, constituting the *Lesser Vehicle* of the initial law.

The four *Fu* are:
1. **Taiyuan (Great Origin)** – An auxiliary to the Dunzhēn.
2. **Taiping (Great Peace)** – An auxiliary to the Dunyuan.
3. **Taqing (Great Clarity)** – An auxiliary to the Dunshén.
4. **Zhengyi (Orthodox Unity)** – Where the three *Dun* and three *Fu* ultimately converge.

The seven divisions correspond to the seven sections of the *Yunji Qiqian* (Cloudy Satchel’s Seven Signatures), each aligning precisely. Within these divisions, subcategories include:
- **Original Texts (Benwen)**
- **Divine Talismans (Shenfu)**
- **Jade Precepts (Yujue)**
- **Numinous Diagrams (Lingtu)**
- **Records (Lu)**
- **Canons (Jielü)**
- **Rites and Etiquette (Weiyi)**
- **Methods and Arts (Fangshu)**
- **Miscellaneous Records (Jizhuan)**
- **Praise and Eulogies (Zanmeng)**
- **Tables and Memorials (Biaoshou)**

The work itself is arranged according to the *Thousand-Character Text*, with each character representing a casefile. Each casefile contains its respective volume count, beginning with *Tian* (Heaven) and ending with *Qun* (Crowd) for the original canon, and from *Ying* (Eagle) to *Jiang* (River) for the Ming-era additions. Each entry includes explanatory annotations, following the format of the *Chongwen Zongmu* (Comprehensive Catalog of the Palace Library) and *Junzai Dushu Zhi* (Reading Notes from the Junzai Studio). Many of the listed works are compilations to fill volumes, such as:
- Liu Mao’s *Easy Arithmetic (Yishu)*, *Hooked Mirror Diagram (Gouying Tu)*, *Lost Commentary on the Nine Affairs (Yushi Shilu)*
- Zhang Li’s *Inner and Outer Commentaries on the Yi Symbols (Yixiang Tu Shu)*
- Lei Sizhi’s *External Variations on the Yi (Yi Wai Bie)*
- *Yi Sui Tongbian* (Comprehensive Variations on Divination)
- *Yi Tu Tongbian* (Comprehensive Variations on Yi Diagrams)

**Annotations:**
- The *Mu Tianzi* (Mysterious Sovereign) entry was originally classified under *Riji Zhu* (Imperial Records).
- The *Shanhai Jing* (Classic of Mountains and Seas) was originally classified under *Dili* (Geography).
- The *Taiyuan Jing* (Great Origin Scripture), *Shouzi Huangji Jingwei* (Emperor Shou’s *Jingwei* Scripture), and *Bao Yunlong Tianyuan Fawei* (Bao Yunlong’s *Tianyuan Revelations*) were originally classified under *Rujia* (Confucianism).
- The *Mozi* was originally classified under *Mojia* (Mohism).
- The *Suwen* (Plain Questions), *Lingshu* (Spiritual Pivot), *Eighty-One Difficult Questions (Baiyi Nan Jing)*, *Sun Simiao’s Thousand-Gold Prescriptions (Qianjin Fang)*, *Ge Hong’s Emergency Handbook (Zhouhou Beiji Fang)*, *Emergency Rescue Prescriptions (Jiujiu Xianfang)*, *Xianzhuan* (Transmissions of the Immortals), *External Surgery Secrets (Waike Mifang)*, *Yuan Zongxian’s Herbal Extensions (Bencao Yanyi)* were originally classified under *Yijia* (Medicine).
- *Gongsun Longzi* and *Yin Wenzi* were originally classified under *Mingjia* (Logicians).
- *Han Feizi* was originally classified under *Fajia* (Legalism).
- *Sunzi* was originally classified under *Bingjia* (Military Strategy).
- *Zhuangzi*, *Yugongzi*, *Luguanzi*, *Huainanzi*, *Zihuazi*, and *Liuzi* were originally classified under *Zongjia* (Miscellaneous Writings).
- *Ji Yiji* (Record of the Strange) and *Jianghuai Yiren Lu* (Records of Strange Men from Jianghuai) were originally classified under *Xiaoshuo* (Fiction).
- *Huangdi Zhaijing* (Yellow Emperor’s Residence Scripture), *Longshou Jing* (Dragon’s Head Scripture), *Jingu Yuheng Jing* (Golden Coffin and Jade Balance Scripture), *Yuan Nü Jing* (Primordial Woman Scripture), *Tongzhan* (Comprehensive Omens), *Daxiang Lijing* (Great Symbol Star Scripture), and *Lingqi Jing* (Numinous Chess Scripture) were originally classified under *Shushu* (Divination and Numerology).
- *Tao Hongjing’s Huayang Jitu* (Huayang Miscellany), *Shouzi Jirang Ji* (Emperor Shou’s *Jirang* Collection), and *Wuyun Zongyuan Ji* (Wuyun’s Comprehensive Source Collection) were originally classified under *Biji* (Miscellaneous Collections).

Though some classifications may seem forced or altered, the compilation retains no genuine Daoist works. Many texts from other traditions were appropriated to bolster the Daoist canon, a practice not worthy of deep scrutiny. While Baiyun Xi’s annotations lack exhaustive detail, they provide a broad outline. This compilation serves as a comprehensive survey of Daoist origins.

The final section, titled *Qunzi* (Crowd), appends a *Catalog of Lost Daoist Canon Texts* in two volumes, though many entries remain incomplete or scattered.

Examining the *Han Dynasty Bibliographic Treatise (Hanshi)*, Daoist texts were recorded as thirty-seven volumes under *Daojia* (Daoist School) and ten volumes under *Shenxianjia* (Immortalist School), originally distinct traditions. Later adherents, dissatisfied with the quietism of *qingjing* (emptiness and tranquility), exaggerated their esoteric practices with elixir formulas and talismans, rebranding themselves as Daoists while truly belonging to the Immortalist school.

Though *Huang-Lao* (Yellow Emperor-Laozi) learning was conflated in the Han, those emphasizing *Dao-De* (Way and Virtue) invoked Laozi, while those emphasizing *lingyi* (numenous anomalies) invoked the Yellow Emperor—both falsely attributing their works to Laozi under the guise of the Yellow Emperor’s authority. Their fabrications were deemed unworthy of scholarly discussion by Confucians, yet their titles persisted in historical records. Thus, their general outlines are preserved here for reference.

**Compiled in the first month of the forty-sixth year of the Qianlong era (1781).**

**Chief Compilers:**
Memorialist Ji Yun
Memorialist Lu Xixiong
Memorialist Sun Shiyi

**Chief Proofreaders:**
Memorialist Lu Feidi

**General Preface**

The **First Section on the Dao of Perfect Reality (洞真部)** emanates from the Supreme Sovereign of the Primordial Heaven (元始天尊), bearing the title *Scriptures of Perfect Reality (洞真经)*, and constitutes the **Great Vehicle’s Supreme Law**, embodying the **Nine Saints’ Dao**. Its divisions comprise twelve categories:

1. **Fundamental Texts (本文)**—the *Book of the Three Origins and Eight Prohibitions (三元八防之书)* and the *Long Narrative of Origins (长行缘起之说)*, serving as the foundational precepts and examples of scriptural teachings.
2. **Divine Talismans (神符)**—inscriptions of *Dragon Script (龙章)* and *Mystic Symbols (灵迹符书)*, establishing the conventions of sacred characters.
3. **Jade Precepts (玉诀)**—as exemplified by *River Master Gong’s Commentary on the Dao-De and the Golden Book (河上公注释道德解金书)*.
4. **Sacred Diagrams (灵图)**—such as the *Encompassing Mirror of the Five Emperors (含景五帝之象图)* and the *Triune Unity Diagram (三一之形)*.
5. **Genealogies and Records (谱录)**—including the *Chapter on the Birth of the Three Sovereigns (生神章所述三君之本行)* and the *Manifestations of the Five Emperors (五帝之示形)*.
6. **Precepts and Statutes (戒律)**—regulating the restraint of the *Six Emotions and Ten Evils (六情十恶)*.
7. **Ritual Etiquette (威仪)**—encompassing *Fast Rituals, Canonical Protocols, Petitions for Scriptures, and Ceremonial Norms (斋法典式请经轨仪)*.
8. **Methods and Practices (方法)**—preserving the *Three Guards, One Regulation (存三守一制)*, *Restrictions on Servitude (拘防策役)*, *Divine Invocations (祈祷)*, *Rain and Sunshine Petitions (雨旸)*, *Rescue of the Lost (济幽)*, and *Manifestation of the Hidden (度显)*.
9. **Miscellaneous Arts (众术)**—including *Alchemical Transmutation (变丹)*, *Stone Refining (炼石)*, *Form Transformation (化形)*, *Concealment Techniques (隐景)*, *Yin-Yang Numerology (阴阳术数)*, *Herbal Elixirs (药饵)*, and *Nourishment Guidance (导养)*.
10. **Records and Biographies (记传)**—such as the *Dao Sovereign’s Original Vocation (道君本业)* and the *Expeditions of the Yellow Man (皇人往行)*.
11. **Hymns and Praises (赞颂)**—as in the *Ancient Chapters of the Nine Heavens (九天旧章)*.
12. **Petitions and Memorials (表奏)**—including *Six Fast Petitions (六斋启头)*, *Three Prohibitions (三防)*, and *Audiences (请谒)*.

All works attributed to the **Primordial Sovereign’s transmission** are classified under their respective categories.

Its auxiliary section is the **Great Unity Department (太乘部)**.

The **Second Section on the Dao of Perfect Unity (洞乘部)** originates from the **Great Sovereign of the Three Realms (三界医王太上道君)**, titled *Scriptures of Perfect Unity (洞乘经)*, and constitutes the **Middle Vehicle’s Middle Law**, embodying the **Nine True Ones’ Dao**. Its twelve categories mirror those of the **Perfect Reality Section**, with all works attributed to the **Great Sovereign’s transmission** classified accordingly. Its auxiliary section is the **Great Peace Department (太平部)**.

The **Third Section on the Dao of Perfect Spirit (洞神部)** stems from the **Ten-Directional Dao Masters (十方道师) and the Great Sovereign Laozi (太上老君)**, titled *Scriptures of Perfect Spirit (洞神经)*, and constitutes the **Lesser Vehicle’s Initial Law**, embodying the **Nine Immortals’ Dao**. Its twelve categories also align with those of the **Perfect Reality Section**, with all works attributed to the **Great Sovereign Laozi’s transmission** classified thus. Its auxiliary section is the **Great Clarity Department (太清部)**.

Additionally, there exists the **Orthodox Unity Section (正一部)**—the **Orthodox One (正一)**—which unifies all preceding **Three Perfect Sections and Four Auxiliary Departments**, consolidating their prohibitions. Thus, it is said: **Three Perfect Sections, Four Auxiliaries (三洞四辅)**.

*—Detailed Catalog of the Imperial Commissioned Complete Library of the Four Treasuries (钦定四库全书), Daoist Canon (道藏) Volume 1.*

These **Scriptures of the Fivefold Soul’s Treasure for Universal Salvation (灵宝无量度人上品妙经)** were revealed in the **Mid-Heaven of Voidness (中天虚无)**, when the **Mysterious Qi (妙炁)** condensed in the **Eastern Azure (碧落)**, a square expanse of one *zhang* (丈). Their radiance extended in eight directions, resplendent and brilliant. At that time, the **Five Elders of Mount Bó (栢陵五老)** gathered around the **Cloud Seat (云座)**. The **Heavenly Sovereign (天真皇人)** was then commanded to draft a model of the **Eightfold Protections (八防)**, emulating the **True Form (夺真)** and symbolizing the **Hidden Books of All Heavens (隐书)**. This was compiled into the **Fivefold Soul’s Treasure for Universal Salvation (五方灵范)**, which recorded the **Mixed Primordial (混元)** Dao of the **Dragon and Han Dynasties (龙汉)**. It was stored in the **Yùluó Palace (郁罗宫)** and the **Zǐwēi Palace (紫微宫)**, totaling **61 volumes**. The **Sacred Scripture (尊经)** is divided into **12,000 kinds of diagrams and records**, all tracing back to these **Eightfold Protections (八防)**. Thus, it is said: **"To pacify Heaven, stabilize Earth, safeguard the realm, and ensure domestic harmony—there is no calamity it cannot avert, no soul it cannot save, no barrier it cannot break, no transformation it cannot achieve. This is the Dao of the Heavenly Sovereign’s Naturalness (天真自然)."**

Additionally, there is the **Elemental Beginning’s Scripture on Primordial Dao and Virtue (元始说先天道德经)**, **five volumes** in total [*Volume 1 of 5*]. **Sòng Xīzhài Lǐ Jiāmóu (宋息斋李嘉谋)** annotated this **Scripture**, stating that its **3,760 profound secrets** must be cross-referenced with the **Supreme Dao and Virtue Scripture (太上道德经)** to reveal the **Mysterious Keys (妙窍)** of **Dao and Virtue (道法)**. It is said: **"The Dao of Primordial Nature (先天) transcends Reason and Qi (理炁), with its 376 mysteries pertaining to Water and Fire (水火)."**

There is also the **Supreme Inner Secret True Treasury Scripture (无上内秘真藏经)**, **ten volumes** in total [*Volume 1 of 10*]:
- **Scripture of the Displaying Dao (显道品)**
- **Scripture of the Discriminating Three Treasures (辩三宝品)**
- **Scripture of the True Essence (真品)**
- **Scripture of the Blessing (恵泽品)**
- **Scripture of the Liberation (解脱品)**
- **Scripture of the Discriminating Illuminated Dao (辩相明部帙品)**
- **Scripture of the Universal Clarity (普明品)**
- **Scripture of the Displaying Virtues (显功德品)**
- **Scripture of the Admonishing Conduct (诫行品)**
- **Scripture of the Wondrous Virtue (妙德品)**
- **Scripture of the Gathering Immortals (集仙品)**
- **Scripture of the Clear Conduct (明行品)**
- **Scripture of the Ultimate (究竟品)**

This is the **first secret protection** of the **Great Treasury (真藏)**, the **Mysterious Dao (妙法)** of the **Great Vehicle (大乘)**.

Lastly, there is the **Supreme Dao of the Limitless Primordial (太上无极总真)**, the **File of Great Clarity (文昌)**, and the **Perfect Reality Scripture of the Immortals (大洞仙经)**, **four volumes** in total [*Volume 1 of 4*]. This **Scripture** contains **39 chapters**, being the **first of the Golden Books (金书)** of the **Supreme Primordial Sovereign (上元太素君)**. It is also known as the **Scripture of the Three Heavens’ Dragon Book (三天龙书)** and the **Scripture of the Nine Heavens’ Perfect Dao (九天太真道经)**. It was compiled by the **Primordial Qi (元始)** of the **Ten Directions (十方)** and the **Heavenly Sovereign (天王)**.

There is also the **Supreme Scripture of Great Clarity and Perfect Reality (上清大洞真经)**, **six volumes** in total [*Volume 1 of 6*], including **Talismans and Divine Images (符像)**:
The **Great Scripture of Secret Protection (大洞秘防)** contains many **names and residences of the Hundred Deities within the Body (身中百神)**. Each deity’s **born abode, palace divisions, mountain forests, towers, halls, pools, and pavilions** are clearly delineated. The **Great Scripture** emphasizes **embracing the male and guarding the female (守雌抱雄)**, blending the **Hundred Deities (百神)** to ensure their constant presence, each attending to its duties. Cultivating and nourishing one’s own **Divine Qi (神炁)**, chanting and reciting the **Precious Scripture (宝章)**, allows the **Heavenly Sovereign’s True Form (天真)** to descend and merge with the **Deities within the Body (兆身中神炁)**, ultimately achieving the **Dao of Everlasting Life (长生不死)**.

Finally, there are **eight volumes under the Solar category (日字号)**.

The **Great Scripture of the Jade Cavern** [*Dadong Yujing*] **[contains two volumes with talismans]**
**[If one practices and upholds the talismans and spells within the Scripture with sincere devotion, refining and blending the spirit while daily renewing, reversing aging, restoring youth, and attaining everlasting longevity—examining the *Divine Records of Immortals* and *Accounts of Ascended Worthies*, those who practiced the *Great Scripture of the Jade Cavern* and ascended to immortality are countless.]**

The **Thirty-Six Sacred Scriptures of the Most High** **[totaling six volumes]**
**[The twelve *Upper Clarity Scriptures*—*Scripture of Mysterious Perfection*, *Scripture of the Dao of Great Unity*, *Scripture of the Mysterious Grove*, *Scripture of Transformation*, *Scripture of the Immortal*, *Scripture of the Yellow Grove*, *Scripture of the Highest Truth*, *Scripture of the Dao Practice*, *Scripture of the Highest Refinement*, *Scripture of Supreme Virtue*, and the *Scripture of the Dao and Its Virtue*—are contained within the hidden treasury of the *Great Jade Clarity Realm*. They are uncorrupted, unspoiled, neither generated nor extinguished, serene and eternally abiding, encompassing all wondrous gates.]**

**[The twelve *Cavernous Mysteries*—*Scripture of the Primordial Yang*, *Scripture of the Primordial Hour*, *Scripture of the Great Calamity*, *Scripture of the Inner Hearing*, *Scripture of the Chain of Life*, *Scripture of the Sacred Secret*, *Scripture of the Dissolution of Demons*, *Scripture of the Heatless*, *Scripture of the Massage*, and *Scripture of the Highest Communication*—are contained within the hidden treasury of the *Great Cavernous Clarity Realm*. They are subtle and pure, forming the root of all heavens and the foundation of all existence.]**

**[The twelve *Great Clarity Scriptures*—*Scripture of the Piercing Vision*, *Scripture of the Gathering of Immortals*, *Scripture of the Cavernous Abyss*, *Scripture of the Inner Secret*, *Scripture of the True One*, *Scripture of the Gathering of Spirits*, *Scripture of the Central Essence*, *Scripture of the Boundless*, *Scripture of the Gathering of Palaces*, and the *Scripture of the Yellow Court*—are contained within the hidden treasury of the *Great Clarity Realm*. They rescue life and transcend death, serving as the vessel for all teachings. These three *Clarity* treasures, profound and true, display named traces and reveal all wondrous gates, encompassing all without exclusion, entering the finest subtleties. Thus, the Three Caverns are divided into the Thirty-Six Sacred Scriptures.]**

**Record of the Mei Mountain Observatories [One volume]**
*(Compiled by Daoist Master Yang Zhiyuan of the Immortal Altar Observatory)*
**[Mei Mountain Immortal Altar Observatory is located in Fengcheng County, Xuanfeng Township, Nanqi Village. Mei Xianjun (Immortal Lord Mei) once concealed himself there. Mei Xianjun was originally from Henan Shouchun Prefecture, surnamed Fu, with the given name Zizhen. During the reign of Emperor Cheng of the Western Han Dynasty, he was entrusted with the governance of Hongzhou Nanchang County. Endowed with a pure and upright nature, he despised worldly affairs and initially retreated to Jiling Mountain to practice cultivation. Later, he was harassed by a ghostly apparition (shiguai) and moved to Jianjiang’s Xiling Mountain. One day, auspicious clouds and divine qi enveloped the peak, and upon opening his door, he saw a Daoist Master, Kongdongjun, descending to dwell there. Thus, he received the Dao/Way from Mei Jun. Afterward, he practiced cultivation for a thousand days, achieving external corporeal transcendence (shenyou) and his inner elixir light (dan guang) illuminating the sky. He attained Dao/Way, ascending to the Cloudly Rank (Yunwei) and verified as an Immortal. The verified traces of his Daoist attainment, imperial decrees, inscribed steles, transmitted records, and poems are all compiled within this text.]**

**Record of the Golden Peaks and the Red Pine Mountain of Jinhua [One volume]**
**[Jinhua Mountain: Red Pine Child (Chisongzi) manifested illusory forms to lure him away from worldly dust, seeking the Dao/Way through symbolic practices (xiangwang) and elixir refining. Remnants of his cultivation include the Elixir Foundation (Danji), Elixir Furnace (Danzao), Elixir Well (Danjing), and the Elixir-Refining Mountain. The Cavern Heaven of Leisurely Play (Youyou Dongtian) has the Stone Chamber Cavern (Shishi), the Lying-in-State Chamber (Woqiang), and the Rock Chamber (Yanshi). The following mountains also have traces: Youshan, Daizhushan, Shishishan, Luoluoyan, Liu Daoyan, Hupingshan, Taoyuan, and Qingshuitan. Additionally, there are the Treasures of the Observatories (Baoji Guan), Jinhua Guan, Yunchao An, and Taicheng Dian, along with steles for the Two Sovereigns (Erhuangjun), Huotian Zhenren, Shishi Xian Guan, Danshan Xian Guan, and Yuntai Guan. Marvelous accounts of ancient True Immortals, divine beings, landscapes, cavern heavens, and inscribed names, along with collected poems and steles, are recorded here.]**

**Record of the Immortal Domain [One volume]**
*(Compiled and gathered by Shoushan Minor Wei Chen Xingding of the Yuxu Tiantai)*
**[Xiantu Mountain, anciently named Jinyun Mountain. According to Daoist texts, it is the twenty-ninth of the Thirty-Six Cavern Heavens (Dongtian), known as the Immortal Domain of Xiantu. The mountain is encircled by 300 li of divine qi. Emperor Huangdi ascended on a Fire Dragon from its peak. The mountain has a Stone House (Shiwu) at its summit, traditionally said to be the Cavern Heaven’s gate. The mountain’s hidden names vary, including Dufeng Mountain, Buxu Mountain, and Tongzi Peak. It features the Concealed True Cavern (Yinzhen Dong), Water Immortal Cavern (Shuixian Dong) at its foot, and the following caverns: Jinlong Dong, Tiantang Dong, Shuanglong Dong, Wangui Dong, Chuangyang Valley, Fuhu Yan, Xiangluan Feng, Lingguishi, beneath the Glazing Stream (Lianxi), Xiaopenglai, Xianjie Yan, Tian Shi Yan, Dongyou Yan, Ditiyun Dong, Dinghu Danjing. Additionally, there are ancient poems and steles inscribed by True Immortals, divine beings, and mortals, along with records of mountain waters and cavern heavens.]**

**Record of the Tiantai Mountain [One volume]**
**[Kuaiji Tiantai Mountain, towering 18,000 zhang in height and encircling 800 li. It has eight layers and four faces, resembling the division of the Cowherd and Weaver Girl constellations. It corresponds to the Tai constellation above, hence its name, Tiantai. Its other names include Tongbo, Chicheng, Pufu, and Dongcang, all referring to different aspects of the mountain. The Record includes collected poems and writings of True Immortals and Daoists across the dynasties.]**

**Illustrated Classic of the Dragon’s Auspicious Observatories, Yu’s Caverns, and Yangming Cavern Heaven [One volume]**
*(Revised by Song Hanlin Scholar Li Zongtan)*
**[Dragon’s Auspicious Observatories are located 15 li southeast of Kuajixian in Zhejiang. This is the site where the Great Yu explored the divine and obtained the Five Treasures Talisman (Wufu) for flood control. Later, Emperor Huangdi used the elixir of the Dao/Way (Tunjia) to open the mountain, completing the flood control and sealing the scriptures within the caverns. The mountain is also known as Yangming Cavern Heaven.]**

**Collected Poems and Praises of the Four Ming Cavern Heaven and Elixir Mountains [One volume]**
*(Compiled by Canghai Yishou Zeng Jian of Linchuan)*
**[Sisheng Mountain, located in the Eastern Sea, features four caverns that emit light, resembling open windows to the heavens. Locals call it Shichuang (Stone Window) Mountain. Its terrain is coiled and winding, encircling 380 li with 280 peaks, rising 210 zhang in height. It is often enveloped by clouds and mist. Notable sites include Yunshan (Cloud Mountain), Yunshan Shishi (Cloud Mountain Stone House), Pufu (Suspended Waterfall), and the Emperor Huizong’s inscribed stele naming it Danshan (Elixir Mountain) and Chishui (Red Water) Cavern Heaven. The Jinguo (Golden Palace) was established using methods of the alchemists (fangshi), with the Golden Dragon and Jade Tablets still preserved today.]**

**Comprehensive Victory Collection of the Southern Sacred Mountain [One volume]**
**[Nanyue Mountain features the following observatories and halls: Hengyue Guan, Zigai Yuan, Shishou Guan, Huagai Yuan, Shangqing Gong, Yinzhen Yan, Yuanyang Gong, Tianzhen Yuan, Beidi Yuan, Lingxu Gong, Dongling Gong, Zhaoxian Guan, Jiuzhen Guan, Jiangsheng Guan, Jixian Gong, Guangtian Guan, Puxian Guan, Xitai Guan, and Zhixu Lingxu Guan. Each of these sites contains verified accounts of True Immortals, divine beings, and their hidden or revealed deeds.]**

**Divine Mysteries Section**

**Volume of Injuries and Cries: Ten Scrolls**
**The *Tàishàng Lǎojūn* ("Highest Venerable Lord") *Shuō Chángqīngjìng Jīng* ("Sutra of Everlasting Purity and Tranquility") **[This sutra elucidates the essential meaning of "purity and tranquility," instructing one to dwell within the mind’s empty clarity, where the true essence alone reveals itself. Thus, the four elements and the heavens and earth all return to their original state.]**

**The *Tàishàng Shēngshèng Dǒulǎo* ("Venerable Lord of Numinous Combat") *Dàshèng Yuánjūn* ("Great Sage, Primordial Lord") *Běndìng Yánshēng Xīn Jīng* ("Sutra of the Primordial Command for Prolonging Life through the Heart") **[The *Dǒulǎo* (斗姥) is the matriarch of the Northern Dipper stars, ruling over the human face and its seven orifices in correspondence with the heart. She has seven *zhēn* (真) in alignment with the Dipper, and if one can return to the heart, uphold the teachings, and dwell in stillness, the Primordial Sovereign’s true essence will manifest and merge with one’s body.]**

**The *Tàishàng Shēngshèng Běndìng Yánshēng Zhēn Jīng* ("Venerable Lord’s True Sutra of the Primordial Command for Prolonging Life")** **[In the first month of *Huándì* (桓帝) *Yǒngshòu* (永寿) Year 1 (705 CE), the *Tàishàng* descended to *Shǔ* (蜀) and temporarily manifested in *Āng* (昂), presenting the *Tianshī* (天师) *Zhāng Dàolíng* (张道陵) with the *Běndìng Yánshēng Jīng* (北斗延生经) in one scroll. It contains the *fēishén* (飞神) talisman of the Golden Gate, the *bǎoguó níngjiā* (保国宁家) talisman for safeguarding the nation and calming the home, and the *yánlíng yìshòu* (延龄益寿) techniques for extending life and longevity, as well as prayers for averting calamities and invoking blessings. The sutra reveals profound mysteries, leaving nothing unrecorded.]**

**The *Tàishàng Shēngshèng Běndìng Chángshēng Miàojīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Marvelous Sutra of the Primordial Command for Everlasting Life")** **[Shared with the four purity and tranquility sutras in the same scroll, it opens with the supreme marvelous chapter of *Língzhāng* (灵章).]**

**The *Tàishàng Shuō Nándǒu Liùsī Yánshòu Dùrén Miàojīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of the Six Officers of the Southern Dipper for Prolonging Life and Guiding Sentient Beings")** **[With talismans. In the first month of *Huándì* (桓帝) *Yǒngshòu* (永寿) Year 1 (705 CE) during the *Shàngyuán* (上元) hour, the *Lǎojūn* (老君) again appointed *Zhāng Dàolíng* (张道陵) as the *Tianshī* (天师) and revealed this sutra to his disciples: *Zuǒshèng* (左圣) *Zhēn Rén* (真人) *Wáng Cháng* (王长) and *Yòushèng* (右圣) *Zhēn Rén* (真人) *Zhào Shēng* (赵升).]**

**The *Tàishàng Shuō Dōngdǒu Zhǔ* (主) *Hùmìng Miàojīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of the Eastern Dipper Master for Protecting Life")** **[The *Tàishàng Lǎojūn* (太上老君) expounded this for the *Tianshī* (天师).]**

**The *Tàishàng Shuō Xīdǒu Jìmíng Hùshēn Miàojīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of the Western Dipper for Recording Names and Safeguarding the Body")** **[In the second month of *Yǒngshòu* (永寿) Year 2 (706 CE), the *Tàishàng* descended to *Shǔ* (蜀) and expounded this for the *Tianshī* (天师).]**

**The *Tàishàng Shuō Zhōngdǒu Dàkuì Bǎomìng Miàojīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of the Central Dipper’s Great Official for Safeguarding Life")** **[The *Tàishàng* (太上) expounded this in *Yǒngshòu* (永寿) *Zhōngxīng* (中兴) Year (713 CE) to the *Zhēngyī Zhēn Rén* (正一真人).]**

**The *Tàishàng Shuō Zhōngdǒu Dàkuì Zhǎngfú Móshén Zhòu Jīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of the Central Dipper’s Great Official for Commanding and Subduing Demon-Gods")** **[Shared with the five Southern Dipper sutras in the same scroll.]**

**The *Tàishàng Běidǒu Èrshí Zhāng Jīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Twenty-Eight Chapter Sutra of the Northern Dipper")** **[One scroll. It expounds the twenty-eight chapters of the Northern Dipper’s *Yuánshuō* (元统).]**

**The *Tàishàng Lǎojūn Shuō Jiùshēng Zhēnjīng* ("Venerable Lord’s True Sutra for Saving Life").**
**The *Tàishàng Lǎojūn Shuō Xiāo Zāi Jīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra for Dispelling Calamities").**
**The *Tàishàng Tàiqīng Tiāntóng Fángmìng Miàojīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Marvelous Sutra of the Celestial Child for Warding Off Life-Threats")** **[With talismans. Received by the Daoist *Liáng Wùzhēn* (梁悟真) of *Sānmáoshān* (三茅山).]**

**The *Tàishàng Tàiqīng Huánglǎo Dìjūn Yùnléi Tiāntóng Yǐnfàn Xiān Jīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of the Celestial Child of the Supreme Yellow Emperor for Wielding Thunder and Concealing Mystical Incantations").**
**The *Tàishàng Lǎojūn Shuō Ānzhái Bāyáng Jīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of the Eight Yang for Calming the Dwelling").**
**The *Tàishàng Lǎojūn Shuō Bǔxiè Bāyáng Jīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of the Eight Yang for Supplements and Gratitude").**
**The *Tàishàng Shuō Shíliàn Shēngshén Jiùfáng Jīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of the Ten Chains for Invoking Life-Gods and Warding Off Threats")** **[Shared with the seven sutras on saving life in the same scroll.]**

**The *Tàishàng Fēibù Wǔxīng Jīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Five-Star Sutra of the Flying Steps")** **[It preserves the essence of the five stars and annotates the methods of the five *zàng* (脏).]**

**The *Tàishàng Fēibù Nándǒu Tàiwéi Yùjīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of the Flying Steps of the Southern Dipper and the Constellation of the Great Enclosure")** **[Shared with the two Five-Star sutras in the same scroll. It contains the Five-Star talismans for warding off names, the Seven-Star talismans for warding off names, and the Six-Star secret talismans.]**

**The *Huángtiān Shàngqīng Jīnquè Dìjūn Língshū Zǐwén Shàngjīng* ("Supreme Yellow Emperor’s Celestial Scripture of the Golden Gate, Imperial Lord, with Purple Text")** **[One scroll, with talismans. This scripture was received by the Five Elders and the *Shàngzhēn Xiān* (上真仙) from the *Shèngjūn* (圣君) and transmitted to the *Qīngtóng Jūn* (青童君). The *Qīngtóng Jūn* (青童君) used it to teach distant disciples, recording their bone and marrow talismans. Those who possess the celestial register should receive this text.]**

**The *Dòngshén Bādì Miàojīng* ("Marvelous Scripture of the Eight Divine Sovereigns")** **[One scroll, with talismans. It includes the eight precepts for fasting, the minor *Dān* (丹) methods, the *Jūfáng* (拘防) techniques, the *Bàopú Mìyán* (抱朴密言) of the Three Sovereigns, the *Sān Huáng Sān Yī Jīng* (三皇三一经), the *Jiǔ Huáng Tú* (九皇图), the *Jiǔ Huáng Fú* (九皇符), the *Xīchéng Yàojié* (西城要诀), and the *Sān Huáng Tiānwén* (三皇天文).]**

**The *Tàishàng Lǎojūn Nèiguān Jīng* ("Venerable Lord’s Sutra of Inner Observation") **[The essence of inner observation lies in calming the mind and illuminating the heart. When thoughts arise, do not let them distract you; preserve the mind and stabilize the roots, ensuring that *jīng* (精) and *qì* (气) do not scatter. The master of one’s body resides within the heart, and the heart can regulate and command the form and spirit so that they do not stray. Since the heart is the true essence, its transformations are boundless, and thus it has no fixed form.

From the Dao, one receives *mìng* (命), which is called *xìng* (性). The heart’s ability to adapt to circumstances is called *yì* (意). When *yì* (意) gives rise to action, it is called *zhì* (志). Knowing all things is called *zhì* (智); discerning all phenomena is called *huì* (慧). When the heart moves and sustains the body, it is called *fáng* (防); when the heart remains still and steadies the form, it is called *zhǐ* (止). The heart’s essence is blood, its spirit is *qì* (气). When *qì* (气) flows clearly and swiftly, it is called *róng* (荣); when it is turbid and sluggish, it is called *wèi* (卫). The heart encompasses all the hundred spirits, which is called the body; all phenomena are visible, which is called the form. The heart’s inherent darkness is called its *zhì* (质); its adaptability is called its *tǐ* (体). The heart’s varying sizes are called the *qū* (躯); myriad unmeasurable thoughts are called the spirit. The heart’s subtle responsiveness to transformations is called its *líng* (灵). When *jīng* (精) and *qì* (气) enter the body, they are called *shēngshén* (生神); when they depart from the body, they are called *sǐ* (死). Thus, the passage of life is called the Dao.

The Dao is present yet formless, formless yet endowed with sentiment. Its transformations are boundless, its essence penetrates all. When the Dao manifests in the body of a sentient being, it becomes the *shēngmíng* (神明) of the heart. Therefore, to teach one the cultivation of the Dao is to teach one the cultivation of the heart; to teach one the cultivation of the heart is to teach one the cultivation of the Dao.]**

The **Inner Observation Sutra**—*"Do not neglect the living Dao, for it endures eternally."*

**The Heart Sutra of the Most High Lord Lao:**
*"Within, the heart is perfected—true nature abides.
True heart, devoid of dwelling—dwelling, devoid of heart.
Perfected, without attachment—attachment ceases, true emptiness arises.
Emptiness, without abode—abode perfected, this is the perfected heart."*

**The Most High Lord Lao’s Inner Alchemy Sutra:**
*"The Three Vessels’ elixir method—
Above, the Returned Elixir, the Golden Fluid;
Midway, the Spirit Water of the Flower Pool;
Beneath, the Five Metals and Eight Stones."*

**The Most High Lord Lao’s Inner Alchemy *Zhīyī Zhēn Dìng* Sutra:**
*"From Nan Yue’s Seven Precious Mountains, the Regal Flower, the Purple Light Heavenly Mother transmitted:
Action and stillness—two as yin, one as yang.
Two brings transformation; one guards constancy.
Know constancy, awaken clarity—embrace unity, contract with truth.
Natural truth is *zhēn dìng*; light is born."*

**The Most High Lord Lao’s Inner Daily Use Marvelous Sutra:**
*"Inner Daily Use lies in the two *liùshí* [times]—
Always maintain purity and stillness, guard the spirit without obstruction—this is *qīngyī*.
No thought arises—this is *jìngxīn*.
Preserve the spirit, fortify the *jīng*—never let a moment pass without vigilance.
This is Inner Daily Use."*

**The Most High Lord Lao’s Outer Daily Use Marvelous Sutra:**
*"Outer Daily Use values stillness, contentment, and frugality—
Always at ease, always sufficient;
Cautious without worry, enduring without shame."*

**The Most High Lord Lao’s *Rìyuè Hùnyuán Jīng* [The Sutra of the Unified Primordium of Sun and Moon]**

*Kàn* [Heaven] and *Lǐ* [Earth], *Kǎn* [Water] and *Lì* [Fire], yin and yang paired—

Refined within the cauldron, fire as the medicine—
This is the pivotal essence of the divine elixir."*

**The *Hùnyuán Bājǐng Zhēnjīng* [The True Sutra of the Eight Scenes of the Unified Primordium]**
*"[Five scrolls in total, four volumes]*
*Hùnyuán Zhēnrén* [The True Person of the Unified Primordium] said:
*'I question myself, answering matters of principle—
Words cannot exhaust it.
To summarize its teachings, lest students struggle to comprehend,
I thus expound on the roots and origins,
Revealing the secrets of heaven’s hidden great function, great concealment, and great medicine.
The elixir’s three methods are refined:
*Lower Alchemy*—three grades in the *Dàgōng* [Great Work] chapter: *Hǔqiān* [Tiger Lead], *Lóngyōng* [Dragon Mercury];
*Middle Alchemy*—three grades in the *Dàyào Qì* [Great Medicine Qi] chapter: *Lóngqiān* [Dragon Lead], *Hǔyōng* [Tiger Mercury];
*Upper Alchemy*—three grades in the *Jīndān* [Golden Elixir] chapter.
The *Yīnyáng Sānyuán Sìxiàng Wǔxíng* [Three Elements of Yin-Yang, Four Symbols, Five Phases] generate climate and cosmic laws—
When aligned, the *Chíqì* [Breath Work] chapter’s four symbols are complete, yin-yang qi is full, entering *Zàohuà* [Creation].
The *Zàohuà Qì* [Creation Qi] chapter—old supplements young, gathering and nourishing.
The *Zhēnwáng Xíngdìng Mìngqì* [True King’s Movement and Commanding Qi] chapter—
The two qi merge, pouring and binding the *Jīngōng* [Refining Function].
The *Wǔxíng Gèxiàn Běn sè* [Five Phases’ Manifested True Colors] chapter—
Inner and outer correspond, *Dìngjīn* [Fixing Metal] chapter,
*Lìzhū Jiējīndān* [Connecting the Pearl to Form the Elixir] chapter,
*Jīnyè Báigāo Chéngdào* [Golden Fluid and White Paste’s Completion of the Dao] chapter."*

**The *Lǎozǐ Xiàngmíng Jīng* [The Sutra of Laozi’s Sacred Names]**
*"[Five scrolls lost; ten volumes]*
*The Highest Laozi instructed the *Shàngfāng Yánshòu Zhēnrén* [True Person of Upper Extension and Longevity]:
*'In the *Wújí Shìjiè* [World of the Boundless], three hundred twenty celestial sovereigns manifest,
Displaying their sacred names.'*"*

**The Most High Lord Lao’s *Bàofùmǔ Ēnzhòng Jīng* [The Sutra of the Heavy Debt of Filial Piety]**
**And *Tiāndìshàngdì Shuō Bàofùmǔ Ēnzhòng Jīng* [The Supreme Heavenly Emperor’s Sutra on Repaying Filial Debt]**

**The *Mù* [Reverent] Canon—Nine Scrolls.**

**The *Dàodé Zhēnjīng* [True Classic of the Dao and Its Power]**
*"[Upper and Lower Scrolls in one]*
*The Most High Lord Lao, in the *Tiānhuáng* [Heavenly Sovereign] era, was the *Tōngshàng Tiānshī* [Celestial Master of Unified Perfection];
In the *Dìhuáng* [Earthly Sovereign] era, he was *Yǒugǔ Xiānsheng* [Master of the Ancient Valley];
In the *Rénhuáng* [Human Sovereign] era, he was *Pángǔ Xiānsheng* [Master Pangu];
In the *Fúxī* era, he was *Yùhuá Zǐ* [Master Idle Flower];
In the *Shénnóng* era, he was *Dàchéng Zǐ* [Master Great Achievement];
In the *Zhūróng* era, he was *Guǎngshòu Zǐ* [Master Longevity];
In the *Huángdì* era, he was *Guǎngchéng Zǐ* [Master Broad Completion];
In the *Kù* era, he was *Lùtú Zǐ* [Master Recorded Maps];
In the *Yáo* era, he was *Wùchéng Zǐ* [Master Five Achievements];
In the *Shùn* era, he was *Yǐnshòu Zǐ* [Master Longevity];
In the *Xià Yǔ* era, he was *Zhēnxíng Zǐ* [Master True Conduct];
In the *Shāng Tāng* era, he was *Jiǎnzé Zǐ* [Master Sharp Rules];
In the *Shāng Yángjiā* [King Yang Jia] year eighteen, he descended in the womb;
In the *Wǔdīng* year nine, he was born.
In the *Zhōu Xībó* era, he was *Cángshǐ* [Archivist], named *Biànyì Zǐ* [Master of Changing Residence];
In the *Wǔwáng* era, he was *Zhùxià Shǐ* [Historiographer], named *Yùchéng Zǐ* [Master of Nurturing Achievement];
In the *Chéngwáng* era, he was *Jīngchéng Zǐ* [Master of Scriptural Completion];
In the *Kāngwáng* era, he was *Guōshū Zǐ* [Master of the Guo Clansman];
Exiting the pass, he wandered the *Liúshā* [Flowing Sands], then returned to teach *Kǒngzǐ* [Confucius] the rites.
In Heaven, he was *Wángchén Dàodàojūn* [Great Dao Lord Wangchen], with *Zhāngmǎn* [Master Zhang] as his teacher.
Among mortals, he was *Chángzōng Zǐ* [Master Constant Pine].
Indeed, the Most High cultivated the Dao and virtue, hiding himself in namelessness as his aim.
Residing long in Zhou, witnessing its decline, he departed.
At the pass, *Yǐnxí* [Emperor Yi of Shu] said, *'Master, you are about to conceal yourself!*
*Please write a book—upper and lower scrolls—
Explaining the meaning of the Dao and virtue in over five thousand words,
Becoming the progenitor of all sutras.'"*

---
*(Note: Unclear or damaged characters—e.g., , , —were reconstructed based on context or standard Daoist terminology.)*

The *Daode Jing* in its ancient form—**both upper and lower scrolls in one volume**—

The *Xisheng Jing* **[Three scrolls, composed by Emperor Huizong of Song]**
**[In the thirty-ninth chapter of the *Xisheng Jing*, Guan Yin [Emperor Yi of Shu] observed the vast qi and discerned the presence of a great true person from the West. He then purified himself, set up barriers, and went to greet him at his lodging, requesting the transmission of secret teachings. The true person then composed a work of countless words, weaving profound and guarded sayings within the five thousand characters. Its essence lies in attaining the One, while transcendence is but a secondary matter. Thus, it guides all under Heaven and future generations to seek the marvelous, grasp the root, embrace emptiness, and preserve softness.]**

The *Wushang Miaodao Wenzhi Zhenjing* **[One scroll]**

**[Guan Yin, the Grand Officer of Zhou, composed nine chapters:
1. *Yuzhang* [One Character]
2. *Zhuzhang* [Two Characters]
3. *Jizhang* [Extreme/Ultimate]
4. *Fuzhang* [Symbols]
5. *Jianzhang* [Mirror]
6. *Qizhang* [Seventh]
7. *Fuzhang* [Kettle]
8. *Chouzhang* [Plans/Calculations]
9. *Yaozhang* [Medicine]]**

The *Chongxu Zhide Zhenjing* **[Three scrolls]**
**[Lièzǐ, named Yùkòu of Zheng, composed eight chapters:
1. *Tiānrú* [Heavenly Blessing]
2. *Huángdì* [The Yellow Emperor]
3. *Zhōu Mùwáng* [King Mu of Zhou]
4. *Zhòngní* [Master Zhongni/Confucius]
5. *Tāng Wèn* [Tang’s Inquiry]
6. *Lìmìng* [Power and Fate]
7. *Yángzhū* [Yang Zhu]
8. *Shuòfēng* [Discourse on Seals]
The *Chongxu Zhide Zhenren*’s writings were enshrined as the *Chongxu Zhide Zhenjing*.]**

**Totaling six scrolls under the *Zhenzi* [True Character] designation.**

The *Dongling Zhenjing* **[One scroll]**
**[Gēngsāngzǐ, also named Kàngcāngzǐ of Chu, a man of Chen, composed nine chapters:
1. *Quándào* [Complete Dao]
2. *Yòngdào* [Applying the Dao]
3. *Zhèngdào* [Political Dao]
4. *Jūndào* [Prince’s Dao]
5. *Chéndào* [Minister’s Dao]
6. *Xiándào* [Worthy’s Dao]
7. *Shùndào* [Submissive Dao]
8. *Nóngdào* [Farmer’s Dao]
9. *Bīngdào* [Military Dao]
The writings of *Dongling Zhenren* were enshrined as the *Dongling Zhenjing*.]**

The *Nanhua Zhenjing* **[Scrolls One through Five]**
**[Zhuāngzǐ, a man of Song named Zhou with the courtesy name Qiú, born in Fángxiàng County, once served as a lacquer-garden overseer. His learning was boundless, yet he sought the essence, ultimately aligning with Laozi’s teachings. He composed thirty-three chapters, over ten thousand words. The Tang dynasty enshrined his writings as the *Nanhua Zhenjing* under the title *Nanhua Zhenren*.]**

*The Divine Seal [damaged character]*
**Totaling eight scrolls under the *Jiézi* [Pure Character] designation.**

**The Supreme Dao of the Non-Dual**

1. *The Great Dao of the Natural and True One* [First Scroll]
2. *The Fivefold Divine Seal* [Second Scroll]
   **[This Dao is the treasure of the Supreme One, passed down from the *Zǐwēi Fángzhòng* [Purple Enclosure, Overseer of the Multitudes] and held in the *Dàdòng Shì* [Great Cavern Chamber]. It is the Way of the Yellow Emperor, received as the *Tàiyǐ Dìjūn* [Great Unity Emperor], ascending to the Celestial Immortal’s Dao.]**

**The Supreme Lord Laozi’s *Yì* [Benefit] Divine Seal and Marvelous Scripture** [One Scroll]
   **[Containing the *Tānjù Lùwén* [Greed-Repelling, Wealth-Accumulating Scriptures], *Liánwǔ Pò* [Modesty-Destroying, Martial Virtue-Breaking Scriptures], *Qīxīng Mìfú* [Seven-Star Secret Seal], *Sān Tāi Huàgài Bǎofú* [Three Palaces’ Celestial Canopy Treasure Seal], and the secret methods of recitation, carrying, and wearing seals.]**

**The Supreme Lord Laozi’s *Hùnyuán* [Chaotic Primordium] Threefold Seals** [Three Scrolls]
   **[Including: the *Dōujiàng Fú* [Master Carpenter Seal], *Jiěhuò Fú* [Dispelling Calamity Seal], *Ānzhái Fú* [Securing the Dwelling Seal], *Bìtǔ Qìfú* [Warding Off Soil *Qi* Seal], *Yímì Fú* [Translocation Seal], *Bìhuǒ Fú* [Warding Off Fire Seal], *Zhǐ Fánghào Fú* [Ceasing Depletion Seal], *Tiánzhòng Fú* [Field Cultivation Seal], *Lìcán Fú* [Silkworm Benefit Seal], *Bǎiguài Fú* [Hundred Demons Seal], *Fángshēn Fú* [Body Defense Seal], *Hànè Fú* [Warding Off Calamity Seal], *Jīguài Fú* [Chicken Demon Seal], *Yángshēng Fú* [Life Extension Seal], *Bì[damaged character] Fú* [Warding Off [damaged character] Seal], *Ānfáng Fú* [Securing Defense Seal], *Bìwēn Fú* [Warding Off Plagues Seal], *Chǎndàn Fú* [Childbirth Difficulty Seal], *Bǎijiě Fú* [Hundred Remedies Seal].]**

**The Non-Supreme Three *Yuán* [Primordial Elements] Pacifying Dwelling and Sacred Talismans** [One Scroll]
   **[The Pacifying Dwelling Talismans, held to assist the *Zhèngqì* [Rectified *Qi*] of Heaven and Earth, and to aid the nation and the times.]**

**The Upper Clarity, Celestial Elixir *Sān Qí* [Three *Qi*] Jade Sovereign’s Six *Chén* [Hours] Flying Halter and Master of Fate’s Great Register** [One Scroll]
   **[The method of deploying the *Nándǒu Fēishén* [Southern Dipper Flying Gods].]**

**The Jade Precepts** [damaged character]
   **[Male Seal] Counting Six Scrolls.**

「**The *Dà Míng* [Great Ming] *Tàizǔ* [Founding Ancestor] *Gāohuáng* [High Emperor] *Yuèzhì* [Imperially Authored] *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue/Power True Classic] [Scroll Four of One]**
   **[This commentary is annotated to align with the *Xiūqí Zhìpíng* [Refinement, Harmony, Governance, and Peace] preface, which states: "Only by knowing this Classic is it the ultimate root of all things, the supreme teacher of the sovereign, and the treasure of the people. It is far beyond the arts of alchemy. Indeed, the Founding Ancestor was the sage ruler of ten thousand generations, and he also revered the Dao/Way and Virtue/Power to this extent."]**
   **Effective Seal, Ten Scrolls**

**Tang *Zōng* [Ancestor] Emperor’s *Yuèzhì* [Imperially Authored] *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue/Power True Classic] Annotation [Scroll Ten of One]**
   **[This section elucidates each chapter and verse, exhaustively probing *lǐ* [principles] and *xìng* [nature], closing off external influences, stifling speculative thoughts, and emphasizing the practical implementation of *quánzuòwàng* [sitting-forgetting, a meditative practice], discarding illusions, and minimizing actions to achieve *wúwéi* [non-action]. It also discusses the rectification of the body and the cultivation of nature.]**
   **Talented Seal, Eight Scrolls**

**Tang *Zōng* [Ancestor] Emperor’s *Yuèzhì* [Imperially Authored] *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue/Power True Classic] Commentary [Scroll Four of One]**
   **[The imperial annotations to the eighty-one chapters, with six scrolls of commentary. Internally, they focus on the fundamentals of self-cultivation; externally, they provide methods for governing the nation.]**

**Annotations of the *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue/Power True Classic] [Scroll Four of One, *Héshàng Gōng* [Master of the Riverbank] Chapter-by-Chapter Commentary]**
   **[This Classic originally comprised two sections—*Shàngjiēng* [Upper Classic] and *Xiàjiēng* [Lower Classic]. After *Héshàng Gōng* [Master of the Riverbank] divided it, there became eighty-one chapters: the *Shàngjiēng* [Upper Classic], which follows Heaven’s *tīanshù* [Heavenly numbers], has thirty-seven chapters; the *Xiàjiēng* [Lower Classic], which follows Earth’s *dìshù* [Earthly numbers], has forty-four chapters.]**

**Commentary on the *Dáodé Jīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue Classic] [Two Scrolls, *Chéngyìláng* [Attendant of the Imperial Secretariat] *Chén Xiànggǔ* [Chen Xianggu] Commentary]**
   **Overlapping Seal, Ten Scrolls**

   **[A compilation of ancient commentaries on defense and governance, with many references drawn from *Nánhúá* [Southern Blossoms, i.e., *Zhuāngzǐ* [Chuang Tzu]) and the *Yìjīng* [Book of Changes].]**
   **Necessary Seal, Eight Scrolls**

**Commentary on the *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue/Power True Classic] [Scroll Four of One, *Wúgōng Lù Xīshēng* [Lu Xi Sheng of Wu Commandery]]**

**Commentary on the *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue/Power True Classic] [Scroll Four of One, *Zìzhèngdiàn Dàxuéshì Lǚ Huìqìng* [Lu Huiqing, Grand Academician of the Zizheng Palace]]**
   **[It discusses the interplay of *yīnyáng* [yin and yang], movement and stillness, understanding the times, and fully realizing the Dao/Way, blending cultivation of the self with governance of the nation.]**
   **Changing Seal, Eight Scrolls**

**The *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue/Power True Classic] *Sānjiě* [Three Commentaries] [Scroll Four of One]**
   **[Composed by *Yùbīnzǐ Dèng Tuó* [Deng Tuo, the Jade Guest]. The inner commentary consists of three elucidations: the first is a *Jiějīng* [Exegesis of the Classic], which adjusts the punctuation and adds or omits one or two fictional characters to reveal the true meaning of each chapter, making its intent clear and harmonious as if naturally born from Heaven, without flaws or errors. The second is a *Jiědào* [Exegesis of the Dao/Way], directly expounding the primordial Dao/Way of Heaven and Earth, its beginning and end, and aligning it with the numbers and principles of the Classic. The third is a *Jiědé* [Exegesis of Virtue/Power], which explores the interplay of *qiántǎo* [precelestial, i.e., Heaven] and *kūn* [the earthly, i.e., Earth], reversing yin and yang, and balancing the Five Phases—Wood, Fire, Earth, Metal, Water—through *jié gōng* [mercury, i.e., the volatile essence], *níng yán* [lead, i.e., the solid essence], one dynamic and one static, all converging with the great Dao/Way. In total, there are over fifty thousand words, titled *Sānjiě* [Three Commentaries].]**

**Direct Commentary on the *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue/Power True Classic] [Scroll Four of One]**
   **[Composed by *Běnlái Zǐ Shào Ruòyǔ* [Shao Ruoyu, the Original Guest]. This commentary states that when the text speaks of *dé* [virtue], it refers to practices rooted in Confucianism; when it speaks of the great Dao/Way, it aligns with the emptiness and stillness of Buddhist teachings. It uses both Confucian and Buddhist perspectives as verification, synthesizing the *Dáodé* [Dao/Way and Virtue] into a unified school. This commentary further includes techniques for retaining form and dwelling in the world to achieve longevity, methods for safeguarding one’s family and ensuring its prosperity, and profound insights for transcending birth and death and perpetually abiding in the Dao/Way.]**

**Commentary on the *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue Classic] [Scroll Four of One, *Shīmǎ Shì* [Sima Family] Abbreviated Commentary]**
   **Obtaining Seal, Ten Scrolls**

**Commentary on the *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue Classic] [Scroll Four of One, *Shānyáng Wáng Bì* [Wang Bi of Shan Yang] Commentary]**
   **[This commentary elucidates the principles of *yīnyáng* [yin and yang].]**

**Commentary on the *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue Classic] [Scroll Four of One, *Méishān Sū Chè* [Su Che of Mei Shan] Commentary]**
   **[This commentary focuses on insights into *xìng* [nature].]**

**New Commentary on the *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue Classic] [Scroll Four of One]**
   **[By *Lǐ Yuē* [Li Yue]. It speaks of *qīngjìng* [purity and stillness], *fēixīn* [flying heart, i.e., meditation], and *wúwéi* [non-action] to preserve the nation.]**
   **Capable Seal, Ten Scrolls**

**Commentary on the *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue Classic] *Zhǐguī* [Guide to the Essentials] [Scrolls Six to Thirteen of One, Missing One Scroll]**
   **[Composed by *Yán Jūnping* [Yan Junping]. This commentary originally discussed the interplay of *xíngqì* [form and *qi*], extending to the subtleties of *shénmíng* [spirit and enlightenment], the origins of *xìngmìng* [life and fate], and the sprouting of *qíngyì* [emotions and intentions]. It further explores the principles of advance and retreat, response and interaction, breathing, bending and extending, all in accordance with Heaven and Earth, and the transformations of *yīnyáng* [yin and yang]. It exhaustively examines the beginning and end of all phenomena, revealing the profound and subtle essence of natural spontaneity, and elucidates the intricate and divine *shényì* [divine principles] with great breadth. The commentary is exceedingly comprehensive.]**

**Commentary on the *Dáodé Zhēnjīng* [Dao/Way and Virtue Classic] *Fángyì* [Defense Meaning] [Scrolls One to Seven of One]**
   **[Commentary by *Song Huìzōng* [Revered Ancestor of Song] and *Wāngchéng* [Wang Cheng], a *Tàixiānshēng* [Senior Student]. This section annotates each verse, incorporating the principles of *Zhuāngzǐ* [Chuang Tzu] and *Yìjīng* [Book of Changes] for verification.]**
   **Forgetting Seal, Seven Scrolls**

**Dao/Way and Virtue *Fángyuán* [Defense Primordial Elements] [Two Scrolls]**
   **[By *Lǐ Dàochún* [Li Daochun], the *Qīng’ān Yīngmǎnzǐ* [Qing’an Yingmanzi]. This commentary systematically annotates the original text, verse by verse, to clarify its meaning. It also elucidates the essentials of rectifying the *yán* [primordial], nourishing the *shén* [spirit], and cultivating the *qi* [vital essence]. Additionally, it summarizes the principles of each chapter to reveal the sequence of probing origins and exhausting sources. At the end of each chapter, it offers praise to fully illuminate the path of self-cultivation and realization of nature. The commentary encompasses all aspects of refining harmony, governing peace, and the fundamental principles of defense—from the most expansive to the most minute, from the profound to the subtle—leaving nothing unaddressed.]**

The *Exposition Beyond the Words* [言外经防] may either: exhaustively clarify through the text, or reverse the language to illuminate the Classic, or use metaphors to elucidate the Dao, or invert the phrases to reveal profundity, or conceal meaning within the sentence, or leak subtlety beyond the words, or indicate meaning before the text, or manifest the profound within the intent. Thus, it is collectively termed *Exposition Beyond the Words* [言外经防].]**

*Tongxuan [通] True Scripture Annotation* **[Scrolls One to Twelve, by Mo Ranzi [默然子]’s Annotation]**
**【Wenzi [文子], surname Xin [辛], given name Ji [钘], also known as Ji [计], a native of Kuiqiu [葵丘] and Pu County [濮上人]. His master was Laozi [老君], and he early heard the Great Dao [大道], compiling twelve chapters titled *Wenzi*. These traced back to the *Taoist Canon* [太上], systematically expounding the Dao of Heaven and Man [天人之道], the suitability of changes through time [时变之宜], and gathering all ancient wisdom into one chapter. It is indeed a pivotal work for the ages. During the Later Tang [后唐], there was a recluse, Xu Lingfu [徐灵府], who secretly cultivated in Hengshan [衡岳] and annotated *Wenzi*. When he presented it, he was granted the title *Tongxuan [通] True Person* [真人], and his work was named *Tongxuan [通] True Scripture*.】**

*Dongling [洞灵] True Scripture Annotation* **[Three Scrolls, by He Can [何灿]]**
*Fei [非] Scrolls, numbered twelve volumes*

*Tongxuan [通] True Scripture Praising Its Meaning* **[Scrolls One to Twelve, by Du Daojian [杜道坚]]**
**【Within the *Inner Scripture* [内经], the term "Laozi" [老子] is often used at the beginning of chapters to honor the Master. This reflects the practice of recording and reciting Laozi’s words at the time, hence not daring to use his own name. The twelve chapters total 180 verses. This commentary interprets them freely, adding 81 more verses. It categorizes the chapters and titles them *Praising Its Meaning*.】**

*Taoist Canon [太上] Laozi [老君] Explains the Scripture of the Primordial Dao* **[Annotations and Explanations, One Scroll]**
**【He Mingzi [合明子], hidden in Zhi [芝] and named Neixiu [内秀], annotated it. This includes the *Primordial Dao Upper Scroll* [元道上篇], *Primordial Dao Middle Scroll* [元道中篇], *Primordial Dao Lower Scroll* [元道下篇], as well as the *Qi Cultivation Method* [兼行气法], *Qi Refining Method* [飬气], and *Qi Drawing Method* [引气等法].】**

*Taoist Canon [太上] Explains the Five Kitchens Scripture* **[Annotations, One Scroll]**
**【Tang Scholar Xiao Ming [唐京萧明] and Yin Zheng [愔] annotated it. This scripture’s five chapters all focus on the essentials of nurturing the body and preserving health. It contains a single profound meaning that can lead one to divine absorption, forgetfulness of the body, and tranquility. It states: "One breath harmonizes with the Great Oneness [太和], and if preserved, the five viscera will be filled, the five spirits will be tranquil; the five viscera filled, flavors will be abundant; the five spirits tranquil, desires will be eliminated." This scripture is the foundation for the five viscera. Just as one seeks food in the kitchen, it is called the *Five Kitchens*.】**

*Taoist Canon [太上] Illuminates the Nine Volumes of the Soul’s Diagram [灵图]*

**The Three Elements’ Ascending Stars and the Golden Scriptures of the Prohibited Crown [三元飞星冠禁金书玉箓图, One Scroll]**
*[The Celestial Master [太上老君] bestowed upon the Heavenly Teacher Zhang Daoling [天师张道陵] at He Mountain [鹤山] the Golden Scriptures inscribed with the Jade Sashes, including the Five-Star Crowned Method [冠五星法], the Seven-Fight Crowned Method [冠七斗法], the Five-Fight Method [冠五斗法], and the Nine Palaces’ Fighting Array [九宫斗诀].]*

**The Five-Fight and Triple Unity Diagram of the Upper Pure Gold Gate Emperor [上清金阙帝君五斗三一图诀, One Scroll]**
*[The oral transmission of Zhou Jun [周君] includes the method of guarding the Five-Fight True Unity, all relying upon visualization techniques of ascending the spirit and piercing the Dipper.]*]

**The Four Qi’s Diagram of Life-Nurturing [四气摄生图, One Scroll]**

**The *Yán* Collection [严字号]**
*Respectful Master Song Guanfu and High Virtue Scholar Xie Shouhao’s Treatise on the Most High Laozi, the Origin of the Dao/Way and Root of the Three Talents, Who Adapts Teaching to the Circumstances and Has Been the Teacher of All Ages, Manifesting and Concealing in Both Existence and Nonexistence, Beyond Defense and Measure. Thus, He Manifests His Teachings in the World, His Traces Revealed as Clearly as the Sun and Moon—How Could Such a One Be Without Record? Fortunately, High Virtue Scholar Xie Jun has thoroughly researched the *Dragon’s* Compilation of Daoist Masters, the *Dragon’s* Transmission of Daoists, and compiled it into **Eight Hundred Twenty Chapters**, titled **Mixed Primordial Sacred Chronicles**.*

---
**The *Jìng* Collection [敬字号]**
*Ten Volumes*
**Brief Chronology of the Most High Laozi [太上老君年谱要略]**
*Compiled by Xie Shouhao of Yongjia. This chronology examines the Most High Laozi’s descent into the world, his title as the Master of the Universal (通天天师), and his lineage from the Three Sovereigns and Five Emperors, serving as teacher to the kings of all dynasties—from the Three Sovereigns to the Five Emperors, the Xia, Shang, Zhou, Qin, Han, Jin, and Song dynasties—down to the present. This work records His illustrious deeds and chronology.*

**The Most High Laozi’s *Golden Book* Preface [太上老君金书内序]**
*[Included in the same volume as the *Brief Chronology*]*

**A Concise History of the Most High Mixed Primordial Laozi [太上混元老子史略]**
*Three Volumes, Compiled by Xie Shouhao*
*[Speaking of the Most High Laozi, who responded to the age and governed the world, serving as the teacher of the Upper Three Sovereigns, the Middle Three Sovereigns, the Lower Three Sovereigns, and the Five Emperors. From the beginning of creation until the time of Yu and Shun, His teachings were unbroken, spanning over **Two Hundred Seventy-Five Thousand Eight Hundred Forty Years**. The Most High Laozi once commanded the deities of Ruanwei Mountain and the divine emissary Yi to transmit to Yu the *Golden Book*, detailing the methods of flood control and the principles of ruling the world and unifying the heavens. This chronicle is compiled to record such events.]*

**The *Dragon’s* Compilation [犹龙集]**
*[Volumes One through Six]*
*[Left Street Prefect and Assistant Censor for Teaching Affairs, Master Jia Shanyuan of Revered Virtue and Awakened Truth, compiled this work. Within, it states that the Most High Laozi, originating from the beginningless, inheriting the natural Dao/Way, revealed His true form, and established the lineage of teachers. Across countless ages, He guided the creation of heaven and earth, nurtured the sacred and the divine. This work includes the *Dragon’s* Transmission of Daoists, the *Dragon’s* Compilation of Sacred Scriptures, the *Dragon’s* Record of the Most High’s descent as the teacher of emperors, His birth years, the clear lineage of seventy-two transformations and eighty-one virtues, and the pillars of history. It also encompasses the *Two Classics of Virtue and Power* (道德二篇) and other essential texts, all of which are meticulously chronicled within.]*

**Facts of the Three True Masters of Fuhou Mountain and Fuqiu Wang Guo [华盖山浮丘王郭三真君事实]**
*[Volumes One through Six]*
*[Fuhou, who played with the Yellow Emperor and the Master of Contained Vitality (容成子) in the Zhou era, transmitted the Dao to the King of Zhou’s heir, Prince Jing of the Han Dynasty, and taught poetry to Shengong (申公). He was also a friend of the King of Chu and bestowed the Dao upon Wang Bao. Thus, he was the ancient Fuhou Gong. The two true masters, Wang and Guo, were originally from Chenliu, Henan (汴州陈留). Guo was the distant cousin of Wang Zefang Ping, who was a descendant of the Wang family. The records of their ascension, their deeds in guiding mortals, and their illustrious transformations are detailed here. This work also includes decrees of praise from successive dynasties, biographies, inscriptions, images, poems, and canonical texts, totaling **Six Volumes and Sixty Chapters**.]*

**上清金液神丹经** [*Three Scrolls, with a preface by the Orthodox Celestial Master Zhang Daoling*]
[*Upper Scroll: The text of the Golden Elixir God-Dan Scripture—ancient writings of unclear meaning, rendered into Han characters by the Dark Lord, totaling 540 characters, expounding on the God-Dan. Middle Scroll: The Immortal True Man of Obscurity compiles methods for refining various elixirs. Lower Scroll: Bao Pu records and compares elixir methods from within the Four Seas and beyond the Eight Wastes, distinguishing and clarifying their differences.*]

**太清石壁记** [*Three Scrolls, compiled by Master Chu Ze*]
[*Includes: The Golden Essence God-Dan Formula, the Great Return Elixir Formula, the Yellow Emperor’s Nine Cauldrons Elixir Formula, the Six-One Clay Method, the Flying Elixir Taboos, the Flying Elixir Fire-Inspiring Auspicious Day Invocation Method, the Flying Elixir Warding Method, the Stone Sulfur Elixir Method, the Eight-Stone Elixir Formula, the Five Spirits Elixir Formula, the Eight Immortals Elixir Formula, the Three Messengers Elixir Formula, the Warding Elixir Method, the Cinnabar Frost Method, the Gold-and-Silver Powder Methods, the Inner Elixir Crafting Method, the Sulfur Water Refinement Method, the Iron Elixir Method, the Dawn Glow Elixir Method, the Radiant Day Elixir Method, the Ascending Sky Elixir Method, the Stalactite Refinement Method, the Iron Powder Crafting Method, the Disease-Treatment Method, the Eight-Stone Elixir Consumption Method, the Water-Refined Mica Method, and the Secret Essentials of the Elixir Scripture with Oral Precepts.*]

**太清金液神气经** [*Three Scrolls*]
[*On the God-Qi: the true Water and Fire, formless yet substantial, void yet natural. Through method, it is summoned and gathered—within the cauldron, medicinal substances arise spontaneously.*]

**太清经天师口诀** [*One Scroll*]
[*On external elixir marvels and methods involving lead and mercury.*]

**太清修丹秘诀** [*One Scroll*]
[*Includes: Methods for gathering elixir seeds and refining with Soul-Sand, the Great Medicine True Lead Precepts by Chong Xu Zi, the Two Separations and Two Uses Method.*]

**温字号计十卷**

**黄帝九鼎神丹经诀** [*Scrolls One to Twenty, compiled by Gu Gang Zi*]
[*Missing the preface; on the origins of God-Dan, methods for selecting a teacher, receiving precepts without relying on true immortals, preserving the spirit and body, dwelling in mountains, warding off evil spirits, beasts, and pests, constructing furnaces, the Five Peaks and Three Platforms Methods, the Iron Gong and Bronze Gong Methods, the Earthen Tripod Method, the Six-One Clay Method, the Red Earthen Tripod Method, the Yellow Clay Sealing Method for the Elixir Cauldron, the Elixir Tripod Coating Method, the Oyster Shell Method, the Elixir Furnace Stabilization Method, the Clay Application Method, the Clay Mixing Method, the Blending Method, the Vinegar Method, the Pounding Method, Gu Gang Zi’s Immortal Cauldron Method, the Cauldron Yellow Sulfur Method, the Yellow Lead-Stone Water Method, the Yellow Pearl Method, the Two Essences and Six-One Method, the Hundred Steams and Nine Flights Method, the Elixir Sand Water Method, the False Separation Method for Lead-Stone Water, the False Separation Method for Crude Saltpeter, the False Separation Method for Martial Salt, the False Separation Method for Stone Bile, the False Separation Method for Stone Spleen, the False Separation Method for Eastern Wild Saltpeter, the Quick-Completion Water Method, the Various Water Methods, the Three-Refined Alcohol Method, the Thirty-Six Formulas for Proper Gold and Silver Refinement, the Auspicious Consumption Methods, the Water-Gold Ladle Method, the Post-Ash Residue Consumption Method, the Stone Bile Essence Extraction Method, the Elixir Adjustment and Refinement Method, the Magnetite Refinement Method, and various other marvelous formulas.*]

**凊字号计九卷**

**九转灵砂大丹资圣经** [*One Scroll*]
[*The True Parents of Soul-Sand Great Elixir (First Chapter), the Sacred Embryo Producing Earth (Second Chapter), the Jade Pool White Lotus (Third Chapter), the Immortal Palm Moonlit Pool (Fourth Chapter), the Purple Palace Golden Lotus (Fifth Chapter), the Purple Palace Surging Spring (Sixth Chapter), the Seven Returns of Golden Elixir and Return Elixir (Seventh Chapter), the Nine-Refined Gold Elixir (Eighth Chapter), and the Fire-Stage Methods.*]

**张真人金石灵砂论** [*One Scroll, by Zhang Yinju of Lu Mountain*]
[*On Gold, Black Lead, Realgar, Cinnabar, True Mercury, Orpiment, Transmutation into Gold, Explanation of Purple Powder, Explanation of Return Elixir, Explanation of Golden Elixir, Explanation of Yin-Yang.*]

**魏伯阳七返丹砂诀** [*Annotated by the Yellow Boy Lord*]
[*Contains ten verses on elixir sand medicinals.*]

**太极真人九转还经要诀** [*Same scroll as the Elixir Sand Precepts*]
[*Formulas: The Yellow Emperor’s Four-Fan Powder, the Queen Mother’s Four Youthful Attendants Powder, Master Mao’s Five Varieties of Reishi Powder, and others.*]

**大洞炼真宝经修伏灵砂妙诀** [*One Scroll, by the Heng Mountain True Man Chen Shaowei (zi Ziming)*]
[*On refining and subduing Soul-Sand: Seven Returns in Seven Chapters, Two Chapters on Gold Elixir, and sequential fire-stages and medicinals.*]

**太洞炼真宝经九还金丹妙诀** [*One Scroll, by the Heng Mountain True Man Chen Shaozheng (zi Ziming)*]
[*On refining mercury: Two chapters, divided into nine grades. The upper three grades extract sand and refine mercury, subdue gold, and blend medicinals into seven chapters. The middle three grades briefly discuss the four yellows and the gold of the five stones. The lower three grades blend the Great Elixir, forge the furnace and cauldron, regulate fire-stages, and verify true elixir attainment—all arranged within the nine grades of the two chapters.*]

**太上卫灵神化九转丹砂法**
[*First Transformation: Refining elixir sand into mercury.
Second Transformation: Reverting mercury into elixir sand.
Third Transformation: Refining elixir sand into mercury again.
Fourth Transformation: Refining the Great Yang flowing cinnabar into elixir sand.
Fifth Transformation: Entering the Yin-Yang furnace to harden the medicinal sand.
Sixth Transformation: Converting hardness into subdued fire yellow silver.
Seventh Transformation: Converting yellow silver into red lead-gold.
Eighth Transformation: Converting red lead-gold into gold powder.
Ninth Transformation: Crafting the Radiant Powder Method.*]

**九转灵砂大丹**
[*Includes: Roasting Soul-Sand Method, Furnace Construction Method, Cauldron Casting Method, Sand Ascension Method, Sand Boiling Method, Silver Vermilion Child Crafting Method, First Transformation True Elixir Method, Second Transformation Pure Yang Elixir Method, Third Transformation Absolute True Elixir Method, Fourth Transformation Marvelous Soul Elixir Method, Fifth Transformation Water Immortal Elixir Method, Sixth Transformation Penetrating Elixir Method, Seventh Transformation Treasure Ceremony Elixir Method, Eighth Transformation One Treasure Elixir Method, Ninth Transformation Ascending True Elixir Method, and the Washing and Dripping Method.*]

**九转青金灵砂丹** [*Same scroll as the God-Transformed Elixir, external elixir*]

**阴阳九转成紫金防化丹诀** [*On the God-Dan*]

「玉洞大神丹砂真要诀」 [*The True Essentials of the Great Divine Elixir of Soul-Sand from the Jade Cavern*]
[*Same scroll as the God-Dan*]

「灵砂大丹秘诀」 [*The Secret Essentials of the Great Soul-Sand Elixir*]
[*One scroll*]
[*Both the Embracing-One Sacred Embryo Soul-Sand Method and the Nine-Transformed Soul-Sand Elixir Method are discussed here as the Great Elixir.*]

「碧玉朱砂寒林玉树匮」 [*The Treatise on Jade and Cinnabar of the Cold Forest and the Jade Trees*]
[*One scroll, compiled by Master Chen of Western Shu*]
[*Discusses mixed preparations of silver, lead, sand, and mercury, as well as methods for divine elixirs and their ingestion.*]

**As per the numbering convention:**
「**A**字号计十卷」
   **大丹记** [*The Great Elixir Record*]
   [*By Wei Boyang*]
   [*Includes: The Mouth-Initiation Method of the Great Primordial Elixir, the Measure of Medicinal Ingredients, the Fire-Heat Method, the True Lead and True Mercury Method, the Medicinal Preparation Method, the Cauldron Method, the Post-Elbow Method.*]

   **丹房湏知** [*The Humid Secrets of the Elixir Chamber*]
   [*Same scroll as the Great Elixir Record*]
   [*By Master Wu of the High-Covered Mountain, a natural man (天然子), and Wu’s Awakening*]
   [*Discusses selecting companions, choosing locations, constructing elixir chambers, taboos, digging elixir wells for true soil, building ash pits, adding water, blending incense, erecting altars, collecting lead, and other methods—all pertaining to the divine elixir.*]

「**B**字号计九卷」
   **药石尔雅** [*The Pharmacopoeia of Medicinals and Stones (Yàjiā)*]
   [*Upper and Lower scrolls, collected by Guang Mei Biao*]
   [*Explains the hidden names of various medicinals and the alternate names of different elixirs.*]

   **丹房奥论** [*The Profound Discussions of the Elixir Chamber*]
   [*One scroll*]
   [*By Xuánhuán (学仙子) Chéng Yīliǎo (程了一着)*]
   [*Includes: 1. The True Soil and Common Soil, 2. The True Lead and Common Lead, 3. The True Mercury and Common Mercury, 4. The Three Sands, 5. The Three Sovereigns, 6. The Three Whites, 7. The Use of Lead, 8. The Use of the Mother (矾), 9. The Method of Borrowing, 10. The Method of Transformation, 11. The Method of Pouring and Dripping, 12. The God-Dan Method, 13. The Ash and Frost Method, 14. The Smoke and Coal Method, 15. The Preparation of Powdered Ingredients—all discussing external elixir methods.*]

   **指归集** [*The Compilation of Refined Methods*]
   [*One scroll*]
   [*By Master Wu of the High-Covered Mountain, Wu’s Awakening*]
   [*Discusses external elixir medicinals and stones.*]

「**C**字号计十一卷」
   **诸家神品丹法** [*The Divine Elixir Methods of Various Masters*]

[*Attributed to the Supreme Above-Imperial (太上以上皇) in the first year of the era *Dingmǎo* (丁卯, 1077 CE) of the *Yuanfù* (元符) reign, and ending in the first year of the era *Guǐchǒu* (癸丑, 1118 CE) of the *Wújí* (無極) reign; this is the record of the Daoist Master Zhou Xi (周師), who departed westward. It is the work of the *Yellow Valley* (豫谷) Sage, Master Gu (郭子), Master Zhang (張天師), and the *Celestial Immortal Elder* (天仙翁) and others, who compiled various era names to align with human temporal cycles. **Dao/Way Canon Classification**

**Jí-zì Category** [*Ten scrolls*]
*Dao/Way Precise Jade Box: Lingbao Gathering of the Dao/Way* [*Three scrolls; on divining the kingly qi*]
**Supreme Dao/Way: Lingbao Three-One-Five Qi True Scripture** [*This scripture was once held by Huangdi of Xuanxuan, who failed to grasp the essence of the Three-One True Qi. After ascending Fengshan, he met the Purple Palace Master and received the inner texts of the Three Sovereigns. Later, he encountered Guangchengzi and obtained the Natural Scripture, yet he still did not comprehend the True One texts of the Three Sovereigns. Xiwangmu preserved this scripture within the Five Cities, with twelve pavilions of Daoist lodgings as outer defenses. The text was inscribed with purple jade and sealed with golden tablets, marked with the *Danchi* light grass and stamped with the Supreme Dao/Way’s central chapter. Those without Daoist registration were forbidden to know of it.*]
**Supreme Dao/Way: Pure and Quiet Jade Character Marvelous Scripture** [*Pure and Quiet Jade Text*]
**Lingbao Scripture of the Celestial Pass** [*Shared with the Five Qi and Three Scriptures*]
[*The Celestial Pass is the belt encircling the Eight Poles, suspending the earth and traversing the heavens, driving the sun and moon, commanding the stars, inhaling and exhaling the Six Jia, governing the heavens and earth, summoning winds and rains, and stirring thunder and lightning. With the mind, one opens the heavens and aligns with the Dao/Way, connecting heaven and earth.*]

**Upper Clarity: Scripture of the True Child’s Inner Transformation and Union with the Jade** [*East Hua’s Preservation of the Dawn Dao/Way; Huangdao Jun transmitted it to those who cultivated the Dao/Way. One observes inwardly with mind and eyes, merging spirit and soul, ascending to commune with the light of the sun and moon, inwardly visualizing the external influx of divine qi, sealing the divine to attract qi, merging with the sun and moon’s radiance, and nurturing the *Dantian* to spontaneously generate the *Zhiying*—the jade flowers and blossoms.*]

**Upper Clarity: Scripture of the Divine Treasure’s Secret Chamber True Name** [*Also named the *Qingtong Daojun’s Recorded Scripture* or the *Taibao Jade Scripture*. Those who cultivate it attain the Upper Clarity’s True Dao/Way. In the Wei dynasty, Jun Hua stored it and transmitted it to Xu Jun, who resided in the Western City Wall, guarding the *Zijie* and *Zijing* with ten *Huayi* and *Yuege* stars. He inscribed it with *Xingyun* and *Baoxiao*, the soaring phoenix’s brocade, and presented it to the Upper Clarity. For a century, it was passed down to True Persons, never revealed to the common people. Thus, the Dao/Way’s brilliance was made manifest in the world.*]

**Lingbao Scripture of the Nine True Persons’ Five Refinements and Three Returns to the Dao/Way’s Observance Gate** [*Shared with the *Inner Transformation* and three other scriptures. The text states: The first refinement is the *Five Secrets*—knowing the Five and illuminating the Ten Actions, entering the *Gate of No Deceit*. The second is observing the mind’s wisdom, penetrating the *Gate of Impermanence and Transformation*. The third is cultivating trust and virtue, resolving the *Gate of Contending with Fate and Returning to Stillness*. The fourth is attaining the subtle essence, entering the *Gate of the Mysterious Root and True Illumination*. The fifth is contracting with the Dao/Way, ascending to the *Gate of Transcendent True Illumination and Verification*. This is called the Five Refinements. If one follows and cultivates, the body and mind become perfectly illuminated, and the Three Treasures naturally return.*]

**Supreme Dao/Way: Longwen Great Cavern Lingbao’s Supreme Secret Marvelous Scripture**
**Supreme Dao/Way: Longwen Great Cavern Lingbao’s Supreme Secret Marvelous Scripture—Exposition** [*Shared with the *Supreme Marvelous Scripture*]
**Upper Clarity: Secret Dao/Way of the Nine Pure Ones’ Returning Luster and Union with the True Person’s Jade Scripture**
**Upper Clarity: Great Abyss Divine Dragon’s Precious Embryo Ascending the Scene’s Supreme Dao/Way Jade Chapter** [*With talismans shared with the *Jade Scripture*]
**Source of the Dao/Way’s Marvelous Cavern True Continuation** [*Three scrolls: upper, middle, lower; on meridians, orifices, and cavities*]

[*Discusses the *Shenshi* (Divine Chamber), cinnabar and mercury, yin and yang, the Dragon and Tiger, fire alchemy, and medicinal substances—all pertaining to the mysteries of the Primordial and Non-Being. It is the progenitor of the alchemical scriptures.*]

*Ancient Text of the Dragon-Tiger Scripture with Commentary* [*Preserved by the Honorable Scholar Rong Dao*]

---
**Róng-zì Category** [*Eight scrolls*]
*The Book of Changes: Parameters of the Same with Commentary* [*Three scrolls: upper, middle, lower; Zhu Xi’s commentary*]
[*Master Zhu once remarked: “The *Parameters of the Same* originally did not elucidate the *Yijing*. I merely borrowed the method of *Najiapian* (placing the trigrams) to convey the timing of advancement and retreat. Later, I obtained Master Shao’s lineage. Again, he said: ‘Now I see it clearly, but I lack the means to proceed.’ Further, he said: ‘Only now do I grasp the outline, but I lack the ingredients.’ The *Parameters of the Same* is indeed the sacred learning of the Primordial. Master Zhu lamented thus.*]

*The Book of Changes: Parameters of the Same—Divided Chapters and Unified True Meaning* [*Three scrolls; Peng Xiao’s elucidation*]
[*This elucidation primarily uses *Kun* and *Qian* as the cauldron, yin and yang as the handles, water and fire as the alchemical mechanism, the Five Phases as auxiliary functions, true lead as the medicine, and the Dao/Way’s essence as the foundation of the elixir. *Kan* and *Li* represent the male and female, heaven and earth are the parents, and the Eight Trigrams are employed to command the Four Seasons to obtain the medicine. The *Yijing* is used to display the forms, and the words are forgotten.*]

*The Book of Changes: Parameters of the Same—Cauldron Mechanism Song and Mirror Diagram* [*With diagrams*]
*The Book of Changes: Parameters of the Same with Commentary* [*One scroll; Anonymous commentary*]

**Ruò-zì Category** [*Fourteen scrolls*]
*The Book of Changes: Parameters of the Same—Elucidation* [*Three scrolls*]
[*By *Baoyizhi* Chen Xianwei. This elucidation uses *Qian* and *Kun* as the Divine Chamber, the sun and moon as the mechanisms, the sixty-four hexagrams as the alchemical processes, the rising and descending of *Yin* and *Yang* as the pivot, the four hexagrams of *Yin* and *Yang* as the keys, and the Four Seasons and Five Phases as the principles. Internally, one remains still and empty, constantly nurturing the Primordial medicinal substances, summoning and refining the elixir within the cauldron.*]

*The Book of Changes: Parameters of the Same with Commentary* [*Three scrolls; by Chu Huagu*]

Here, the mechanisms are exposed.*]

**The Laws of Distinguishing the Poor and the Rich, The Precepts of Guarding the Three Treasures, The Exegesis of the Teacher’s Guard, The Ancient Precepts of Great and Small Rectitude, The Laws of Originating from Earth, The Precepts of the Upright Minister and Son as Ruler, The Precepts of the Father and Teacher Obtaining Daoist Immortality, The Three Unifications in Harmony, The Precepts of Swiftly Learning the True Dao and Discarding Heretical Texts, The Flying Bright Ancient Precepts, etc.**
